`SymbolTable` (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h, .cc) which implements stat name interning using variable-length byte encoding. The `StatNamePool` class (defined within symbol_table.h) provides a convenient way to add and manage stat names without reference counting. `StatName` objects are lightweight references to interned names in the symbol table.\\n\\n## Scope Hierarchy\\nThe primary implementation of the Stats::Scope hierarchy is in `ThreadLocalStoreImpl` (source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h, .cc). This class implements the `StoreRoot` interface and contains a nested `ScopeImpl` class that extends the abstract `Scope` interface (envoy/stats/scope.h). The scope system supports nested scopes with prefix composition and provides thread-local caching for fast stat lookup. Each scope manages a central cache of counters, gauges, histograms, and text readouts.\\n\\n## Stat Allocation and Metric Implementation\\nThe `AllocatorImpl` class (source/common/stats/allocator_impl.h, .cc) manages the creation and lifetime of stat objects. The `MetricImpl` template (source/common/stats/metric_impl.h, .cc) provides the base implementation for all metrics and uses a `MetricHelper` class to manage stat names and tags. The `HistogramImpl` (source/common/stats/histogram_impl.h, .cc) and `ThreadLocalHistogramImpl` classes provide histogram-specific implementations, with `ParentHistogramImpl` coordinating thread-local histogram merging.\\n\\n## Tag Extraction from Metric Names\\nTag extraction is implemented in two main components:\\n1. `TagProducerImpl` (source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h, .cc) which orchestrates a collection of tag extractors\\n2. `TagExtractorImplBase` (source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h, .cc) and its subclasses which perform regex-based extraction of tags from metric names\\n3. `TagUtility::TagStatNameJoiner` (source/common/stats/tag_utility.h, .cc) which combines stat names with extracted tags\\n\\n## Stat Sink Dispatch System\\nThe `Sink` interface (envoy/stats/sink.h) defines the contract for stat sinks. The `MetricSnapshot` class provides a snapshot of all metrics for flushing. Multiple sink implementations exist:\\n\\n### Statsd-based Sinks\\n- `UdpStatsdSink` and `TcpStatsdSink` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/statsd.h, .cc) - Core statsd implementation with configurable tag formats\\n- Configuration for standard statsd, DogStatsd, and Graphite statsd variants (source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/config.h, source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/config.h, source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/config.h)\\n\\n### Prometheus Support\\n- `MetricsServiceSink` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/grpc_metrics_service_impl.h, .cc) - Implements prometheus format via gRPC metrics service\\n- `MetricsFlusher` class - Handles conversion of Envoy metrics to prometheus client protobuf format (io::prometheus::client::MetricFamily)\\n- The metrics service dispatches metrics to external metrics collection services that support prometheus format\\n\\n### Other Sinks\\n- `HystrixSink` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/hystrix.h, .cc) - Streaming metrics for hystrix dashboard\\n- `OpenTelemetryGrpcSink` and `OtlpMetricsFlusher` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/open_telemetry_impl.h, .cc) - OpenTelemetry metrics export\\n- `WasmStatSink` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/wasm_stat_sink_impl.h) - WASM-based custom sink\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n- `StatsMatcherImpl` (source/common/stats/stats_matcher_impl.h, .cc) - Filters which stats are created/flushed based on configuration\\n- `IsolatedStoreImpl` (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h, .cc) - Standalone stats store for testing and isolated contexts\\n- `CustomStatNamespacesImpl` (source/common/stats/custom_stat_namespaces_impl.h, .cc) - Manages custom stat namespace registration\\n- Null implementations (null_counter.h, null_gauge.h, null_text_readout.h) - No-op stats for disabled metrics\\n- Tag formats (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/tag_formats.h, .cc) - Defines various tag format standards\\n\\n## Public API\\nThe public API is defined in the envoy/stats/ directory:\\n- `allocator.h` - Allocator interface\\n- `scope.h` - Scope interface with methods to create and find metrics\\n- `sink.h` - Sink interface and MetricSnapshot\\n- `store.h` - Store/StoreRoot interface\\n- `stats.h` - Counter, Gauge, Histogram, and related interfaces\\n- `tag.h` - Tag data structures\\n- `tag_extractor.h` and `tag_producer.h` - Tag extraction interfaces\\n\\nThe entire system is designed for high-performance metric collection with minimal contention through thread-local storage and symbol table interning.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1516,"cache_read_input_tokens":71961,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1516},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d18142a6-09b3-43a5-8783-557c1d1463ff","uuid":"1f80680e-7af9-4a86-9090-1b3a91464b84"}

The `HistogramImpl` (source/common/stats/histogram_impl.h, .cc) and `ThreadLocalHistogramImpl` classes provide histogram-specific implementations, with `ParentHistogramImpl` coordinating thread-local histogram merging.\\n\\n## Tag Extraction from Metric Names\\nTag extraction is implemented in two main components:\\n1. `TagProducerImpl` (source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h, .cc) which orchestrates a collection of tag extractors\\n2. `TagExtractorImplBase` (source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h, .cc) and its subclasses which perform regex-based extraction of tags from metric names\\n3. `TagUtility::TagStatNameJoiner` (source/common/stats/tag_utility.h, .cc) which combines stat names with extracted tags\\n\\n## Stat Sink Dispatch System\\nThe `Sink` interface (envoy/stats/sink.h) defines the contract for stat sinks. The `MetricSnapshot` class provides a snapshot of all metrics for flushing. Multiple sink implementations exist:\\n\\n### Statsd-based Sinks\\n- `UdpStatsdSink` and `TcpStatsdSink` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/statsd.h, .cc) - Core statsd implementation with configurable tag formats\\n- Configuration for standard statsd, DogStatsd, and Graphite statsd variants (source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/config.h, source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/config.h, source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/config.h)\\n\\n### Prometheus Support\\n- `MetricsServiceSink` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/grpc_metrics_service_impl.h, .cc) - Implements prometheus format via gRPC metrics service\\n- `MetricsFlusher` class - Handles conversion of Envoy metrics to prometheus client protobuf format (io::prometheus::client::MetricFamily)\\n- The metrics service dispatches metrics to external metrics collection services that support prometheus format\\n\\n### Other Sinks\\n- `HystrixSink` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/hystrix.h, .cc) - Streaming metrics for hystrix dashboard\\n- `OpenTelemetryGrpcSink` and `OtlpMetricsFlusher` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/open_telemetry_impl.h, .cc) - OpenTelemetry metrics export\\n- `WasmStatSink` (source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/wasm_stat_sink_impl.h) - WASM-based custom sink\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n- `StatsMatcherImpl` (source/common/stats/stats_matcher_impl.h, .cc) - Filters which stats are created/flushed based on configuration\\n- `IsolatedStoreImpl` (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h, .cc) - Standalone stats store for testing and isolated contexts\\n- `CustomStatNamespacesImpl` (source/common/stats/custom_stat_namespaces_impl.h, .cc) - Manages custom stat namespace registration\\n- Null implementations (null_counter.h, null_gauge.h, null_text_readout.h) - No-op stats for disabled metrics\\n- Tag formats (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/tag_formats.h, .cc) - Defines various tag format standards\\n\\n## Public API\\nThe public API is defined in the envoy/stats/ directory:\\n- `allocator.h` - Allocator interface\\n- `scope.h` - Scope interface with methods to create and find metrics\\n- `sink.h` - Sink interface and MetricSnapshot\\n- `store.h` - Store/StoreRoot interface\\n- `stats.h` - Counter, Gauge, Histogram, and related interfaces\\n- `tag.h` - Tag data structures\\n- `tag_extractor.h` and `tag_producer.h` - Tag extraction interfaces\\n\\nThe entire system is designed for high-performance metric collection with minimal contention through thread-local storage and symbol table interning.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
